{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01FxPi4LK5YicbtEvhQekzTK","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_017oKuZRwpEpNJrwriu4NLeH","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/numpy/lib/_rolling_median.py","content":"\"\"\"\nRolling median computation.\n\"\"\"\nimport functools\nimport numpy as np\nfrom numpy._core import overrides\nfrom numpy._core.fromnumeric import asarray, asanyarray\n\n__all__ = ['rolling_median']\n\narray_function_dispatch = functools.partial(\n    overrides.array_function_dispatch, module='numpy')\n\n\ndef _rolling_median_dispatcher(a, window_size, *, axis=-1, mode='valid'):\n    return (a,)\n\n\n@array_function_dispatch(_rolling_median_dispatcher)\ndef rolling_median(a, window_size, *, axis=-1, mode='valid'):\n    \"\"\"\n    Compute a rolling median over a 1-D or N-D array.\n\n    Parameters\n    ----------\n    a : array_like\n        Input array or object that can be converted to an array.\n    window_size : int\n        The size of the rolling window. Must be positive.\n    axis : int, optional\n        The axis along which to compute the rolling median. Default is -1 (last axis).\n    mode : {'valid', 'same', 'full'}, optional\n        Determines the output shape and edge handling:\n        - 'valid': Only compute where the window fully overlaps with the array.\n          Output shape is reduced. (default)\n        - 'same': Keep the same shape as the input array. Edge values use\n          partial windows.\n        - 'full': Include all partial windows at both ends. Output is expanded.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    rolling_median_result : ndarray\n        Array of rolling median values. The output shape depends on the mode.\n\n    See Also\n    --------\n    median : Compute the median along an axis\n\n    Notes\n    -----\n    The rolling median is computed by sliding a window of length `window_size`\n    along the specified axis and computing the median of values within each window.\n\n    For edge handling with 'same' mode, the window is centered when possible.\n    For 'valid' mode, the window must completely fit within the array.\n    For 'full' mode, all partial window overlaps are included.\n\n    Examples\n    --------\n    >>> import numpy as np\n    >>> a = np.array([1, 2, 3, 4, 5])\n    >>> np.rolling_median(a, 3)\n    array([2., 3., 4.])\n    >>> np.rolling_median(a, 3, mode='same')\n    array([1., 2., 3., 4., 5.])\n    \"\"\"\n    a = asanyarray(a)\n\n    if not isinstance(window_size, int) or window_size < 1:\n        raise ValueError(\"window_size must be a positive integer\")\n\n    if mode not in ('valid', 'same', 'full'):\n        raise ValueError(\"mode must be 'valid', 'same', or 'full'\")\n\n    # Normalize axis\n    if axis < 0:\n        axis = a.ndim + axis\n    if axis < 0 or axis >= a.ndim:\n        raise ValueError(f\"axis {axis} is out of bounds for array of dimension {a.ndim}\")\n\n    # Handle edge case where window_size is 1\n    if window_size == 1:\n        return a.copy()\n\n    # Get the size along the axis\n    axis_size = a.shape[axis]\n\n    # Handle edge case where window_size > axis_size\n    if window_size > axis_size:\n        if mode == 'valid':\n            # Return empty array\n            output_shape = list(a.shape)\n            output_shape[axis] = 0\n            return np.empty(tuple(output_shape), dtype=a.dtype)\n        elif mode == 'same':\n            # Return full array as all values use partial windows\n            return a.copy()\n        else:  # 'full'\n            # Include all partial overlaps\n            output_size = axis_size + window_size - 1\n            output_shape = list(a.shape)\n            output_shape[axis] = output_size\n            return np.empty(tuple(output_shape), dtype=a.dtype)\n\n    # Compute output shape based on mode\n    if mode == 'valid':\n        output_size = axis_size - window_size // 2)\n                end = min(axis_size, i + (window_size - window_size // 2))\n                window = column[start:end]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n        else:  # 'full'\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                start = max(0, i - Default is -1 (last axis).\n    mode : {'valid', 'same', 'full'}, optional\n        Determines the output shape and edge handling:\n        - 'valid': Only compute where the window fully overlaps with the array.\n          Output shape is reduced. (default)\n        - 'same': Keep the same shape as the input array. Edge values use\n          partial windows.\n        - 'full': Include all partial windows at both ends. Handle edge case where window_size is 1\n    if window_size == 1:\n        return a.copy()\n\n    # Get the size along the axis\n    axis_size = a.shape[axis]\n\n    # Handle edge case where window_size > axis_size\n    if window_size > axis_size:\n        if mode == 'valid':\n            # Return empty array\n            output_shape = list(a.shape)\n            output_shape[axis] = 0\n            return np.empty(tuple(output_shape), dtype=a.dtype)\n        elif mode == 'same':\n            # Compute output shape based on mode\n    if mode == 'valid':\n        output_size = axis_size - window_size + 1\n    elif mode == 'same':\n        output_size = axis_size\n    else:  # 'full'\n        output_size = axis_size + window_size - 1\n\n    # Create output array\n    output_shape = list(a.shape)\n    output_shape[axis] = output_size\n    result = np.zeros(tuple(output_shape), dtype=np.float64)\n\n    # Move the target axis to the first position for easier iteration\n    a_moved = np.moveaxis(a, axis, 0)\n    result_moved = np.moveaxis(result, axis, 0)\n\n    # Reshape for easier iteration\n    original_shape = a_moved.shape\n    a_flat = a_moved.reshape(original_shape[0], -1)\n    result_flat = result_moved.reshape(output_size, -1)\n\n    # Compute rolling median for each column\n    for col_idx in range(a_flat.shape[1]):\n        column = a_flat[:, col_idx]\n        result_column = result_flat[:, col_idx]\n\n        if mode == 'valid':\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                window = column[i:i + window_size]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n        elif mode == 'same':\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                start = max(0, i - window_size // 2)\n                end = min(axis_size, i + (window_size - window_size // 2))\n                window = column[start:end]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n        else:  # 'full'\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                start = max(0, i - (window_size - 1))\n                end = min(axis_size, i + 1)\n                window = column[start:end]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n\n    # Move axis back to original position\n    output_shape_moved = list(original_shape)\n    output_shape_moved[0] = output_size\n    result = np.moveaxis(result_moved.reshape(tuple(output_shape_moved)), 0, axis)\n    return result\n\n\n# Now run tests\ndef test_basic():\n    \"\"\"Test basic rolling median.\"\"\"\n    a = np.array([1, 2, 3, 4, 5])\n    result = rolling_median(a, 3, mode='valid')\n    print(\"Basic test:\")\n    print(f\"  Input: {a}\")\n    print(f\"  Window size: 3, mode: 'valid'\")\n    print(f\"  Result: {result}\")\n    print(f\"  Expected: [2. 3. 4.]\")\n    assert np.allclose(result, [2., 3., 4.]), f\"Expected [2., 3., 4.], got {result}\"\n    print(\"  ✓ PASSED\\n\")\n\ndef test_window_1():\n    \"\"\"Test with window size 1.\"\"\"\n    a = np.array([1, 2, 3, 4, 5])\n    result = rolling_median(a, 1)\n    print(\"Window size 1 test:\")\n    print(f\"  Input: {a}\")\n    print(f\"  Result: {result}\")\n    assert np.array_equal(result, a), f\"Expected {a}, got {result}\"\n    print(\"  ✓ PASSED\\n\")\n\ndef test_mode_same():\n    \"\"\"Test with 'same' mode.\"\"\"\n    a = np.array([1, 2, 3, 4, 5])\n    result = rolling_median(a, 3, mode='same')\n    print(\"Mode 'same' test:\")\n    print(f\"  Input: {a}\")\n    print(f\"  Result shape: {result.shape}\")\n    print(f\"  Result: {result}\")\n    assert result.shape == a.shape, f\"Expected shape {a.shape}, got {result.shape}\"\n    print(\"  ✓ PASSED\\n\")\n\ndef test_mode_full():\n    \"\"\"Test with 'full' mode.\"\"\"\n    a = np.array([1, 2, 3, 4, 5])\n    result = rolling_median(a, 3, mode='full')\n    print(\"Mode 'full' test:\")\n    print(f\"  Input shape: {a.shape}\")\n    print(f\"  Result shape: {result.shape}\")\n    expected_size = 5 + 3 - 1  # Must be positive.\n    axis : int, optional\n        The axis along which to compute the rolling median. Default is -1 (last axis).\n    mode : {'valid', 'same', 'full'}, optional\n        Determines the output shape and edge handling:\n        - 'valid': Only compute where the window fully overlaps with the array.\n          Output shape is reduced. Output is expanded.\n\n    Returns\n    -------\n    rolling_median_result : ndarray\n        Array of rolling median values. The output shape depends on the mode.\n\n    See Also\n    --------\n    median : Compute the median along an axis\n\n    Notes\n    -----\n    The rolling median is computed by sliding a window of length `window_size`\n    along the specified axis and computing the median of values within each window.\n\n    For edge handling with 'same' mode, the window is centered when possible.\n    For 'valid' mode, the window must completely fit within the array.\n    For 'full' mode, all partial window overlaps are included.\n\n    Examples\n    --------\n    >>> import numpy as np\n    >>> a = np.array([1, 2, 3, 4, 5])\n    >>> np.rolling_median(a, 3)\n    array([2., 3., 4.])\n    >>> np.rolling_median(a, 3, mode='same')\n    array([1., 2., 3., 4., 5.])\n    \"\"\"\n    a = asanyarray(a)\n\n    try:\n        window_size = int(window_size)\n    except (TypeError, ValueError):\n        raise TypeError(\"window_size must be an integer\")\n\n    if window_size < 1:\n        raise ValueError(\"window_size must be a positive integer\")\n\n    if mode not in ('valid', 'same', 'full'):\n        raise ValueError(\"mode must be 'valid', 'same', or 'full'\")\n\n    # Normalize axis\n    if axis < 0:\n        axis = a.ndim + axis\n    if axis < 0 or axis >= a.ndim:\n        raise ValueError(f\"axis {axis} is out of bounds for array of dimension {a.ndim}\")\n\n    # Handle edge case where window_size is 1\n    if window_size == 1:\n        return a.copy()\n\n    # Get the size along the axis\n    axis_size = a.shape[axis]\n\n    # Compute output shape based on mode\n    if mode == 'valid':\n        output_size = axis_size - window_size + 1\n    elif mode == 'same':\n        output_size = axis_size\n    else:  # 'full'\n        output_size = axis_size + window_size - 1\n\n    # Create output array\n    output_shape = list(a.shape)\n    output_shape[axis] = output_size\n    result = np.zeros(tuple(output_shape), dtype=np.float64)\n\n    # Move the target axis to the first position for easier iteration\n    a_moved = np.moveaxis(a, axis, 0)\n    result_moved = np.moveaxis(result, axis, 0)\n\n    # Reshape for easier iteration\n    original_shape = a_moved.shape\n    a_flat = a_moved.reshape(original_shape[0], -1)\n    result_flat = result_moved.reshape(output_size, -1)\n\n    # Compute rolling median for each column\n    for col_idx in range(a_flat.shape[1]):\n        column = a_flat[:, col_idx]\n        result_column = result_flat[:, col_idx]\n\n        if mode == 'valid':\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                window = column[i:i + window_size]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n        elif mode == 'same':\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                start = max(0, i - window_size // 2)\n                end = min(axis_size, i + (window_size - window_size // 2))\n                window = column[start:end]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n        else:  # 'full'\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                start = max(0, i - (window_size - 1))\n                end = min(axis_size, i + 1)\n                window = column[start:end]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n\n    # Move axis back to original position\n    output_shape_moved = list(original_shape)\n    output_shape_moved[0] = output_size\n    result = np.moveaxis(result_moved.reshape(tuple(output_shape_moved)), 0, axis)\n    return result\n","numLines":142,"startLine":1,"totalLines":142}}}

window_size + 1\n    elif mode == 'same':\n        output_size = axis_size\n    else:  # 'full'\n        output_size = axis_size + window_size - 1\n\n    # Create output array\n    output_shape = list(a.shape)\n    output_shape[axis] = output_size\n    result = np.zeros(tuple(output_shape), dtype=np.float64)\n\n    # Move the target axis to the first position for easier iteration\n    a_moved = np.moveaxis(a, axis, 0)\n    result_moved = np.moveaxis(result, axis, 0)\n\n    # Reshape for easier iteration\n    original_shape = a_moved.shape\n    a_flat = a_moved.reshape(original_shape[0], -1)\n    result_flat = result_moved.reshape(output_size, -1)\n\n    # Compute rolling median for each column\n    for col_idx in range(a_flat.shape[1]):\n        column = a_flat[:, col_idx]\n        result_column = result_flat[:, col_idx]\n\n        if mode == 'valid':\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                window = column[i:i + window_size]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n        elif mode == 'same':\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                start = max(0, i - window_size // 2)\n                end = min(axis_size, i + (window_size - window_size // 2))\n                window = column[start:end]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n        else:  # 'full'\n            for i in range(output_size):\n                start = max(0, i - (window_size - 1))\n                end = min(axis_size, i + 1)\n                window = column[start:end]\n                result_column[i] = np.median(window)\n\n    # Move axis back to original position\n    output_shape_moved = list(original_shape)\n    output_shape_moved[0] = output_size\n    result = np.moveaxis(result_moved.reshape(tuple(output_shape_moved)), 0, axis)\n    return result\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":92,"oldLines":12,"newStart":92,"newLines":18,"lines":[" ","     # Compute output shape based on mode","     if mode == 'valid':","-        output_size = axis_size -
